csiPlugin (csi_plugin.go) is the main CSI plugin implementing the Kubernetes volume plugin interface. It includes a RegistrationHandler that validates and registers new CSI drivers when they become available. The csi_plugin.go file is responsible for plugin initialization and lifecycle management. The csiDriverClient (csi_client.go) encapsulates the gRPC communication with CSI drivers, implementing the csiClient interface with methods like NodePublishVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, and NodeUnstageVolume for node-side operations. The DriversStore (csi_drivers_store.go) maintains a registry of all CSI drivers installed on the node.\\n\\n**Node Plugin Operations (pkg/volume/csi/)**:\\nThe csiAttacher (csi_attacher.go) implements the Attach/Detach operations, calling the CSI driver's node operations. The csiMountMgr (csi_mounter.go) handles mounting and unmounting of volumes, implementing Setup() and TearDownAt() methods. The csiBlockMapper (csi_block.go) manages block device volumes. The expander.go implements volume expansion operations, and csi_metrics.go provides metrics collection for CSI volumes.\\n\\n**Node Information Management (pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/)**:\\nThe nodeInfoManager (nodeinfomanager.go) registers CSI drivers on nodes by updating both Node and CSINode objects. The Interface defines methods like InstallCSIDriver() and UninstallCSIDriver() that manage the CSINode object with driver information, topology labels, and volume attachment limits.\\n\\n**Attach/Detach Controller (pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/)**:\\nThe attachDetachController (attach_detach_controller.go) is the main controller managing volume attachment and detachment across the cluster. It implements the AttachDetachController interface and coordinates with CSI drivers through the volume plugin interface. The reconciler (reconciler/reconciler.go) executes the attach/detach operations by calling the Attach() and Detach() methods on the csiAttacher.\\n\\n**PersistentVolume Controller (pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/)**:\\nThe PersistentVolumeController (pv_controller.go) bridges CSI operations to the core storage API, handling dynamic provisioning of CSI-backed volumes. The pv_controller_base.go sets up the CSI translator for migrating in-tree volumes to CSI. The provisionClaimOperationExternal() function calls external provisioners for CSI volumes.\\n\\n**Storage API Types (staging/src/k8s.io/api/storage/v1/)**:\\nThe types.go file defines CSIDriver, CSINode, and VolumeAttachment objects that coordinate CSI operations. VolumeAttachment objects capture the intent to attach/detach volumes and track the attachment status managed by external CSI attachers.\\n\\n**Integration Flow**:\\n1. csiPlugin (csi_plugin.go) is the main CSI plugin implementing the Kubernetes volume plugin interface. It includes a RegistrationHandler that validates and registers new CSI drivers when they become available. The csi_plugin.go file is responsible for plugin initialization and lifecycle management. The csiDriverClient (csi_client.go) encapsulates the gRPC communication with CSI drivers, implementing the csiClient interface with methods like NodePublishVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, and NodeUnstageVolume for node-side operations. The DriversStore (csi_drivers_store.go) maintains a registry of all CSI drivers installed on the node.\\n\\n**Node Plugin Operations (pkg/volume/csi/)**:\\nThe csiAttacher (csi_attacher.go) implements the Attach/Detach operations, calling the CSI driver's node operations.
